    Selection of Partners

    Bones and flesh are bright and luminous, the spirit is pure and substantial, and there are flowers worth using. There are five types that are unsuitable: First, the shell type, where the female’s external genitalia resembles a snail shell, winding inward; second, the type with markings, where the female’s genitalia is as small as the tip of a chopstick, only allowing passage but difficult for union, known as the stone woman; third, the drum flower type, which is tight and seems to have no opening; fourth, the horn flower type, which is sharp and pointed; fifth, the vein type, where the meridians have not reached fourteen but appear first, or arrive at fifteen or sixteen, or are unbalanced, or entirely absent. These five types without flowers cannot unite with the sun, how could they possibly form an immortal fetus?

    Union

    Male essence and female blood combine to form a fetus. The child's shape resembles that of the parents, as it has a definite origin. Therefore, those seeking children should have men enhance their essence and regulate their desires, ensuring the Yang path remains strong; women should nourish their blood and balance their energy, allowing for the timely arrival of menstruation, cultivating one another in the process—this is the way to have children.

    For weak men and frail women, the methods of nurturing are what those seeking children must discuss. For a strong man and robust woman, with abundant essence and blood, children will naturally arise, so no supplementation is needed. However, for men who are weak and constantly lack essence, they should strengthen their kidneys to enhance their essence; for frail women, who frequently lack blood, they should strengthen their spleen to nourish their blood. To strengthen the kidneys, one can use the Six Flavors Rehmannia Decoction, with the addition of Schisandra and processed Aconite for cold essence. To strengthen the spleen, one can use the Ginseng, Poria, and Atractylodes Powder, adding Angelica and Chuanxiong if blood is deficient.[24p]

    箴曰：男精充盈，阴血时行，阳变阴合，旺胎妙凝。男益其精，女调其经，乃能有子，螽斯振振。嬴男亏阳，弱女亏阴，虽交不孕，虽孕不成。调养之法，上工所明，不遇其良，反成其灾。　　肥盛妇人无子者，宜服苍附导痰丸。　　妇人无子，或经水不调，自有调经之方。血不足者，莫如六味地黄丸。素有疾病者，莫如补脾参苓白朮散。若夫子宫虚寒者，不可不讲，苟执勿用热药之禁，所谓执中无权，犹执一也。今采韩飞霞女金丹、杨仁斋艾附暖官丸二方，以备治虚寒者之用。[25p]

    A proverb says: When a man’s essence is abundant and the woman’s blood flows regularly, the yang transforms and combines with the yin, nurturing and solidifying the fetus wonderfully. A male strengthens his essence, a female regulates her cycle, only then can they conceive, and the cicadas will buzz. If a man loses his yang or a woman loses her yin, even if they mate, they will not conceive; even if they do conceive, it will not hold. The methods of adjustment and nourishment are clear to the skilled; if they do not encounter the right conditions, it may bring disaster instead.

    For women who are substantial and yet have no children, it is advisable to take the Cang Fu Dao Phlegm Pill. For women without children, or those with irregular menstruation, there are methods to regulate the cycle. Those with insufficient blood should take the Liu Wei Di Huang Pill. Those with pre-existing diseases should take the Bu Pi Shen Ling Bai Zhu Powder. As for those with deficient cold in the uterus, it is crucial to emphasize this: if one insists on avoiding the prohibition of heating medicines, it is akin to being one-sided.

    Now, I recommend the formulas from Han Feixia’s Golden Elixir and Yang Renzhai’s Ai Fu Warm Official Pill for treating those with deficiency and cold.[25p]

    协期篇

    　　种子歌云：三十时中两日半，二十八九君须算。落红满地是佳期，金水过时空撩乱。撩乱之时枉费功，树头树底觅残红。但解花开能给子，何愁丹桂不成丛？此言妇人月经方绝，金水才生，此时子宫正开，乃受精结胎之候，妙合太和之时，过此佳期，则子宫闭而不受胎矣。然男女之分，各有要妙存焉。如月候方绝，一日、三日、五日交会者成男，二日、四日、六日交会者成女，过此则不孕矣。　　诀曰：何为种子法？经里问因由。昨日红花谢，今朝是对周。蓝田种白玉，子午叙绸缪。三五成丹桂，二四白梅抽。此古经水未行之时，血海正满，子宫未开，不能受精以成其娠。经水既行，则子宫开，血海净，斯能受其精矣。昨日，谓两日半后也。子午，谓阴阳初动之始，即复姤二卦，非二时也。[26p]

    Xieqi Poem

    The Seed Song says: “At thirty, two and a half days have passed; on the twenty-eighth and twenty-ninth, one must calculate. Fallen petals cover the ground, marking an auspicious time; the golden water has stirred, causing disorder. In times of chaos, efforts are wasted; one seeks remnants of red among the trees, both high and low. If one understands the blooming of flowers, there’s no worry that the red osmanthus won’t cluster together.”

    This means when a woman’s menstruation has just ended, and the golden water has just begun; at this moment, the uterus opens, indicating the time for conception. It coincides perfectly with the time of harmony. After this auspicious period, the uterus closes and cannot conceive. However, there are unique secrets for men and women. For example, if conception occurs right after menstruation—on the first, third, or fifth day, it results in a boy; on the second, fourth, or sixth day, it results in a girl. Beyond this, there will be no pregnancy.

    The conclusion states: “What is the method for seed? Within the classics, it inquires about the reasons. Yesterday, red flowers fell; today it corresponds to the surrounding. In Lantian, white jade is planted; between noon and midnight, threads of silk weave together. Three and five days yield the red osmanthus; two and four days bring forth white plums.”

    This refers to the time before water in the ancient scriptures; the sea of blood is full, and the uterus has not opened, so it cannot conceive. Once the menstruation has occurred, the uterus opens and the sea of blood is cleared, enabling it to accept the essence. “Yesterday” refers to two and a half days later. “Between noon and midnight” indicates the beginning of the interplay of yin and yang, aligning with the hexagram Jiou, not merely the two times.[26p]

    经止后一日、三日、五日，得奇数为阳，必生男，故曰丹桂成。二日、四日、六日，得偶数为阴，必生女，故曰白梅抽。七日之后，子宫复闭，不成娠矣。　　诀曰：玉湖须浅泛，重载却成忧。阴血先参聚，阳精向后流。血开包玉露，平步到瀛洲。浅泛者，即《素女论》所谓九浅一深之法也。盖男女交媾，浅则女美，深则女伤，故云重载即成忧矣。阴血先聚，阳精后冲，则血开裹精而成男；阳精先至，阴血后参，则精开裹血而成女。即断易天元赋所谓阳包阴则桂庭添秀，阴包阳则桃洞得仙也。　　诀曰：从斯相暂别，牛女隔河游。二月花开发，方知喜气优。好事当传与，谗言莫妄绸。此言种子之后，男子别寝，不可再交，盖精血初凝，恐再冲击也。故古者妇人有娠，即居侧室，以养其胎气也。二月，即次月也。[27p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[27p]

    After the period has ended one day, three days, or five days, if an odd number is obtained, a boy will definitely be born; thus it is said that the red osmanthus blossoms. If an even number is obtained on the second, fourth, or sixth day, a girl will definitely be born; thus it is said that the white plum blossoms. After seven days, the uterus closes again, and pregnancy cannot occur.

    The secret says: The jade lake must be shallow, heavy burdens only bring worries. Yin blood gathers first, while yang essence flows later. When blood opens, it wraps the jade dew, and one steps lightly to Penglai. The shallow approach refers to the method of "nine shallow and one deep" as mentioned in "The Book of the Plain Girl." Thus, in the union of man and woman, if shallow, the girl is beautiful; if deep, the girl is harmed, hence "heavy burdens only bring worries." If yin blood gathers first and yang essence flows later, blood opens to wrap essence and a boy is produced; if yang essence arrives first and yin blood gathers later, essence opens to wrap blood and a girl is produced. This corresponds to the assertion in the "Book of Changes" that yin wraps yang to add beauty to the osmanthus garden, and yang wraps yin for the peach grotto to gain immortality.

    The secret says: From this union, we temporarily part, the cowherd and the weaver girl cross the river to play. In the second month, flowers bloom, one knows the joy has arrived. Good news should be shared, while malicious words must not be carelessly spread. This refers to after the seed is planted, the man should sleep apart, avoiding further intercourse, as the essence and blood are just beginning to coagulate, fearing another impact. Therefore, in ancient times, when a woman became pregnant, she would live in a side chamber to nurture her fetal energy. The second month refers to the following month.[27p]

    前月经行，协期种玉，次月经断，真有娠矣。当此之时，胎教之法，不可不讲，故常使之听美言，见好事，闻诗书，操弓矢，淫声邪色不可令其见闻也。　　箴曰：月事初下，谓之红铅。三十时足。佳期不愆。旧污既去，新癸未生。子宫正开，玉种蓝田。阳道刚健，交接勿烦。勿令气忤，必使情欢。阳偶阴和，雨顺风恬。芳花结子，丹桂森森。　　种子须得天德月德，合三合六合益后续世日吉。正月丁壬丙辛，建成收开闭。二月申巳甲己，建平定危成。三月丁壬，建执成收开。四月辛丙庚乙，建平满成开。五月亥寅丙辛，建成收除。六月甲己，建除满成开。七月癸戊丁壬，建危成收。八月寅亥庚乙，建危成除。九月丙辛，建执破危成。十月乙庚甲己，建平成闭。十一月巳申丁壬，建除执破成。[28p]

    The previous month, when menstruation began, was the time for planting the precious seeds. The next month, when menstruation stopped, signified true conception. At this time, the methods of prenatal education must not be neglected; hence, one should often listen to beautiful words, witness good deeds, hear poetry and literature, and practice archery. It is imperative to avoid lascivious sounds and immoral sights.

    The admonition states: When menstruation first arrives, it is called "red lead," and it lasts for thirty days. The auspicious time is not to be missed. The old impurities have been expelled, and the new beginnings have not yet emerged. The uterus has properly opened, and the precious seeds are sown in fertile fields. The male principle is strong; do not let the process be burdensome. Do not let the energy become discordant; ensure that the emotions are joyful. When the male and female principles unite in harmony, may the rain be timely and the winds be gentle. The fragrant flowers bear fruits, and the red osmanthus flourishes.

    The seeds must receive the blessings of Heaven and Moon, harmonizing the Triple Harmony and the Six Harmonies for a favorable continuation into the future; the days are auspicious. In the first month, Ding, Ren, Bing, and Xin bring about initiation and closure. In the second month, Shen, Si, Jia, and Ji establish stability and resolve dangers. In the third month, Ding and Ren conduct initiation and closure. In the fourth month, Xin, Bing, Geng, and Yi lead to fullness and opening. In the fifth month, Hai, Yin, Bing, and Xin result in initiation, continuation, and removal. In the sixth month, Jia and Ji bring about removal, fullness, and opening. In the seventh month, Gui, Wu, Ding, and Ren culminate in resolution and closure. In the eighth month, Yin and Hai ensure resolution and removal. In the ninth month, Bing and Xin deal with initiation, overcoming dangers, and achieving completion. In the tenth month, Yi, Geng, Jia, and Ji establish peace and closure. In the eleventh month, Si, Shen, Ding, and Ren lead to removal, initiation, and overcoming completion.[28p]

    十二月庚乙，建成开闭。【外建成开闭，俱合天喜，必合益后续世在内。】　　《易》系辞曰：天地絪缊，万物化醇，男女媾精，万物化生。诚哉是言也。男女胥悦，阴阳交通而胚胎结矣。尝观周颂云。思媚其妇，有依其士，则夫妇亲爱之情，虽在田野，未之忘也。故于衽席之间，体虽未合，神已先交，阳施阴受，血开精合，所以有子。苟夫媚其妇，而女心未惬，则玉体才交，琼浆先吐，阳精虽施而阴不受矣。妇依其夫，而士志或异，则桃浪徒翻，玉霜末滴，阴血虽开，而阳无入矣。阴阳乖离，成天地不交之否，如之何其能化生万物哉！　　求子之法，须察妇人经水毕，四旺日之后，子宫方开，可以交合而有子。春甲乙寅卯日，夏丙丁巳午日，秋庚辛申酉日，冬壬癸亥子日，四季戊己辰戌丑未日。如不值其日，取四旺时行之。[29p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[29p]

    In the twelfth month of the Gengyin year, the construction is completed and the gates are opened. [The outer construction opening aligns with the heavenly joy, and it will surely benefit future generations within.] The "I Ching" states: Heaven and Earth unite, and all things transform into essence; men and women merge their vital energies, and all things give birth. Truly, this is an accurate statement. When men and women are both pleased, the interaction of yin and yang brings about the formation of the embryo. Consider the praise in the "Songs of Zhou": When a man cherishes his wife and has the support of his companions, the affection between husband and wife, even in the fields, is never forgotten. Thus, between the mat and pillow, though their bodies may not yet intermingle, their spirits have already connected; the male essence is imparted, and the female receives, leading to conception. However, if the husband delights in his wife yet she is not satisfied, their bodies may touch, the essence may be initially released, but if the female does not receive, conception will not occur. If the wife follows her husband but his will differs, then it is like waves of peaches crashing but the frost of jade has no drop; thus, the female blood may open but there is no entry from the male. When yin and yang are at odds, the conjunction of heaven and earth cannot occur; how then can all things be transformed and birthed? The method for seeking a child requires careful observation: After a woman’s menstrual flow has completed and during the four auspicious days, when her womb is opened, intercourse can occur to conceive a child. During spring on the days of Jia and Yi in the months of Yin and Mao, in summer on the days of Bing and Ding in the months of Si and Wu, in autumn on the days of Geng and Xin in the months of Shen and You, and in winter on the days of Ren and Gui in the months of Hai and Zi, as well as on the days of Wu and Ji in the months of Chen, Xu, Chou, and Wei. If these days are not suitable, one should choose auspicious times to carry it out.[29p]

    《番生经》云：交合之时，女有五伤之候：一者阴户尚闭不开，不可强刺，强刺则伤肺；二者女兴已动欲男，男或不从，兴过始交则伤心，伤心则经不调；三者少阴而遇老阳，玉茎不坚，茎举而易软，虽入不得摇动，则女伤其目，必至于盲；四者女经水未尽，男强逼合，则伤其肾；五者男子饮酒大醉，与女子交合，茎物坚硬，久刺之不止，女情已过，阳兴不休则伤腹。五伤之候，欲求子者，交合之时，不可不慎也。　　男女未交合之时，男有三至，女有五至。男女情动，彼此神交，然后行之，则阴阳和畅，精血合凝，有子之道也。若男情已至，而女情未动，则精早泄，谓之孤阳。女情已至，而男情未动，女兴已过，谓之寡阴。《玉函经》云：孤阳寡阴即不中，譬取鳏夫及寡妇，谓不能生育也。[30p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[30p]

    The "Fan Sheng Jing" states: At the time of union, a woman has five signs of injury: First, if her vagina is still closed and cannot open, forcing penetration could harm the lungs. Second, if the woman desires the man but he does not respond, and if desire surpasses the initial union, it could harm the heart and disrupt the menstrual cycle. Third, if a young yin encounters an old yang, the phallus may not be firm, and if it enters but cannot move, it could harm the woman's eyes, potentially leading to blindness. Fourth, if the woman's menstrual flow has not fully ended and the man forces the union, it could injure her kidneys. Fifth, if a man is heavily intoxicated and engages with a woman, though he is firm and continues for a long time, if the woman has already passed her desire, excessive stimulation could harm her abdomen. These five signs of injury must be taken seriously by those desiring children at the time of union.

    Before men and women unite, there are three conditions for men and five for women. When their feelings are stirred and they connect spiritually before engaging, the yin and yang harmonize, and their essence and blood coalesce, leading to the possibility of conception. However, if the man's feelings have reached their peak while the woman's have not, it results in premature ejaculation, referred to as solitary yang. Conversely, if the woman's feelings are stirred but the man's are not, and she has already passed her peak desire, it is called deficient yin. The "Yu Han Jing" says that solitary yang and deficient yin do not lead to conception, as in the case of a widower and a widow, who are unable to conceive.[30p]

    另有三至者：谓阳道奋昂而振者，肝气至也；壮大而热者，心气至也；坚劲而久者，肾气至也。三至俱足，女心之所悦也。若痿而不举者，肝气未至也。肝气未至而强合则伤其筋，其精流滴而不射矣。壮而不热者，心气未至也。心气未至而强合，则伤其血，其精清，冷而不暖也。坚而不久者，肾气未至也。肾气未至而强合，则伤其骨，其精不出，虽出亦少矣。此男子之所以求子，贵清心寡欲，以养肝心肾之气也。若夫女子有五至者：面上赤起，眉靥乍生，心气至也；眼光涎沥，斜视送情，肝气至也；低头不语，鼻中涕出，肺气至也；交颈相偎，其身自动，脾气至也；玉户开张，琼液浸润，肾气至也。五气俱至，男子方与之合，而行九一之法，则情洽意美。其候亦有五也，娇吟低语，心也；合目不开，肝也；咽干气喘，肺也；两足或曲或伸，仰卧如月，脾也；口鼻气冷，阴户沥出沾滞，肾也。有此五候，美快之极。[31p]

    There are also three signs: the first is when the yang essence is vigorous and vibrant, which indicates the arrival of liver energy; the second is when it is robust and warm, indicating the arrival of heart energy; the third is when it is firm and enduring, indicating the arrival of kidney energy. When all three are present, it brings pleasure to a woman’s heart. If one is weak and cannot perform, it means the liver energy has not arrived. If the liver energy has not arrived and one forcefully engages, it will harm the muscles, causing the essence to flow and drip without being released. If one is strong but not warm, it means the heart energy has not arrived. If the heart energy has not arrived and one forcefully engages, it will harm the blood, making the essence clear, cold, and unwelcoming. If one is firm but not enduring, it means the kidney energy has not arrived. If the kidney energy has not arrived and one forcefully engages, it will harm the bones, and the essence will not emerge, even if it does, it will be minimal. This is why men seek children; it is essential to cultivate a clear mind and few desires to nourish the energies of the liver, heart, and kidneys.

    For women, there are five signs: when the face blushes, and beauty appears, it indicates the arrival of heart energy; when tears appear in the eyes and emotional glances are given, it indicates the arrival of liver energy; when a woman bows her head and does not speak, and there’s dripping from the nose, it indicates the arrival of lung energy; when they embrace closely and the body begins to move on its own, it indicates the arrival of spleen energy; when the jade gate opens, and the precious fluid flows, it indicates the arrival of kidney energy. When all five energies are present, only then can a man unite with her, engaging in the methods of Nine One, leading to harmonious feelings and delightful connections. There are also five conditions to observe: soft murmurs and gentle words, associated with the heart; closed eyes, associated with the liver; dry throat and gasping, associated with the lungs; legs bending or stretching, lying back like the moon, associated with the spleen; and cold breath from the mouth and nose, with fluid dripping from the female organ, associated with the kidneys. With these five conditions, it leads to extreme beauty and joy.[31p]

    男子识其情而采之，不惟有子，且有补益之助。　　男女交媾之际，更有避忌，切须慎之！若使犯之，天地夺其寿，鬼神殃其身，又恐生子不肖不寿之类。谨守戒禁，可以长生，所忌之要，备述于后。　　天地震动　卒风暴雨　雷电交作　晦朔弦望　月煞日破　大寒大暑　日月薄蚀　神佛生辰　庚申甲子　本命之日　三元八节　五月五日　名山大川　神祠社庙　僧宇道观　圣贤像前　井灶前后　火光闹烘　　已上时地禁忌，切须慎之，不可交合。犯之者，令人寿夭，小则生病；或若坐男，令其丑貌怪相，形体不全，灾疾夭寿。　　神力劳倦　愁闷恐惧　悲忧思怒　疾病走移　发赤面黄　酒醉食饱　病体方痊　女子行经　　已上交合禁忌，不可犯之，令人虚损，耗散元气。　　诸所禁忌，敷奏于前，复有五月十八日，是天地牝年之日，阴阳交合之期，世人须避，慎不可行房。[32p]

    When a man understands his feelings and pursues them, not only does he have offspring, but he also gains beneficial support.     The shaking of heaven and earth, sudden storms and heavy rains, the clash of thunder and lightning, the dark and bright phases of the moon, eclipses of the sun, extreme cold and heat, the solar and lunar eclipses, the birthdays of deities and Buddhas, the day of one's birth, the three festivals and eight sections, the fifth day of the fifth month, famous mountains and rivers, shrines and temples, the abodes of monks and Taoists, before the images of sages, and in front of wells and stoves, in the presence of fire’s brilliance — all these times and places are to be treated with caution; one must not engage in union.     犯之重则夺命，轻则减寿。若于此时受胎孕，子母难保。　　夫妇交合之时，三虚四忌，不可不讲。三虚者：谓冬至阳生，真火正伏，夏至阴生，真水尚微，此一年之虚也；上弦前，下弦后，月廓空，此一月之虚也；天地晦冥日月，此一日之虚也。遇此三虚，须谨避之。四忌者：一忌本命正冲，甲子庚申晦朔之日；二忌大寒大暑大醉大饱之时；三忌日月星辰寺观坛庙灶墓之处；四忌触忤恼怒骂詈击搏之事。犯此三虚四忌者，非惟无子，令人夭寿。　　右种子法，见于群书所载者如此，仿而行之，无不验者。虽然，窃有说焉。田野之氓，邪淫之女，多至生育者，竟皆知此种子法耶？盖待其天癸动子户开而构精者，此鸟兽字尾之期，待其男三至女五至而通体者，此阴阳交感之理，其机至微，非文字之所能尽者。况乎田野之氓，其交疏而情易洽，邪淫之女，其思切而情先交，所以阴阳和而育多也。[33p]

    If the offense is grave, it will lead to death; if light, it will shorten one’s life. If conception occurs at this time, both mother and child are difficult to preserve.

    During the union of husband and wife, there are three voids and four prohibitions that must be observed. The three voids refer to: the winter solstice when yang is born but true fire is dormant, and the summer solstice when yin is born but true water is still weak; this constitutes the void of the year; the first quarter before the full moon and the last quarter after the full moon, when the moon is empty; this constitutes the void of the month; the darkening of heaven and earth, the sun and moon; this constitutes the void of the day. When encountering these three voids, one must exercise caution and avoid them.

    The four prohibitions are: firstly, to avoid the day of one’s own heavenly stem in direct conflict, such as the day of the winter solstice and the day of the summer solstice; secondly, to avoid times of extreme cold, extreme heat, excessive drunkenness, or overindulgence in food; thirdly, to avoid places associated with the sun, moon, stars, temples, altars, or graves; fourthly, to steer clear of actions that cause anger, curses, or violence. Violating these three voids and four prohibitions not only results in childlessness but can also lead to premature death.

    The method of seeding mentioned here is documented in various texts; if one follows it, there are no failures. However, I have a different viewpoint. It is common for the common folk in the fields, along with licentious women, to give birth despite possibly being unaware of this seeding method. They wait for the heavenly essence to awaken and open the door to conception, coinciding with the mating seasons of birds and beasts. They wait for males to approach three times and females five times before they achieve their full potential; this is the principle of yin and yang harmonizing, so subtle that words cannot fully express it. Moreover, the common folk display straightforward emotions that easily connect, while licentious women, with their deep thoughts and engaging emotions, facilitate the harmony of yin and yang resulting in higher fertility.[33p]

    妇人秘科 【明　万全】

    　　　　　济阴通元赋

    　　经候既调，男女可合。不出三日之期，宜尽一时之乐。干辟坤合，阳唱阴和。滴秋露于花枝兮，玉粒可结；鼓春风于桃浪兮，金鳞自跃。阴包阳兮则丹桂发芽，阳包阴兮则红莲吐萼。天地之大义，生民之本始。勿谓刍荛之言，作诙谐而笑谑。
    　　　　　种子章

    　　生育者，必阳道强健而不衰，阴癸应候而不想，阴阳交畅，精血合凝，而胎元易成矣。不然，阳衰不能下应乎阴，阴亏不能上从乎阳，阴阳乖离，是以无子。　　种子者，女贵平心定气。盖女子以身事人而性多躁，以色悦人而性多忌，稍不如意，即忧思怨怒矣。忧则气结，思则气郁，怨则气阻，怒则气上，血随气行，气逆血亦逆，此平心定气，为女子第一紧要也。其药饵则宜服乌鸡丸以养其气血，调其经候，斯为得理。若彼桂附丹石，动气耗阳损血消阴之剂，一切远之。　　女人无子，多因经候不调，药饵之辅，尤不可缓。[34p]

    Women's Secret Teachings

    Essence of Yin and Yang

    When the cycle of the menstrual period is regular, men and women may unite. Within three days, one should enjoy the pleasures of the moment. The male yang and the female yin harmonize; when the yang sings, the yin responds. Dew drips from the autumn leaves, and jade-like grains can form; the spring wind blows through the peach blossoms, and golden scales leap naturally. The profound principles of heaven and earth are the foundation of life. Do not dismiss these words as mere idle talk fit for laughter.

    Seed Chapter

    For conception, the male must be robust and not diminished, while the female must be responsive and not averse; when yin and yang flow harmoniously, essence and blood unite, facilitating the formation of the fetus. Otherwise, if the yang is weak, it cannot align with the yin; if the yin is deficient, it cannot respond to the yang. Separation of yin and yang leads to childlessness. The essence of seed lies in a woman maintaining a calm heart and steady spirit. Indeed, as women serve others with their bodies, they often become anxious, desiring approval based on their beauty. At the slightest displeasure, they may feel worry, resentment, or anger. Worry binds the qi, thought causes stagnation, resentment obstructs qi, and anger raises it; blood flows with the qi, and if qi goes astray, the blood follows. Therefore, maintaining a calm heart and steady spirit is of utmost importance for women. As for medicinal remedies, they should take black chicken pills to nourish qi and blood and regulate their cycles, which is the correct approach. One must stay away from excessive remedies that deplete yang and consume blood, as these are detrimental. Childlessness in women is often due to menstrual irregularities; thus, support through medicine is especially critical and should not be delayed.[34p]

    若不调其经候而与之合，徒用力于无用之地，此调经为女人种子紧要也。　　女子素有浊漏带下之疾，经水不调，不能成胎，谓之下元虚惫，不能聚血受精，宜补虚濇脱，用前乌鸡丸、补官丸调之。　　妇女阴质，取象于月。若自朔至望，经水行不失其候者，结胎易，生子多寿，以月光渐生，月轮渐满也。若自望至晦，经水行或失其期者，胎难结，生子多夭，如月光渐消，月廓渐空也。此造化之理，可与懵者道耶？　　凡种子者，当应候之时，男服补肾益精之药，女则调其饮食，淡其滋味，避其寒暑，至于夜半生气乘旺之时，依三至五至三虚四忌行之，自然交而必孕，孕而必成矣。[35p]

    If one does not regulate the menstrual cycle and align with it, but instead expends effort in unproductive areas, this regulation of the cycle is crucial for women’s fertility.     The female reproductive quality is emblematic of the moon. If from the new moon to the full moon, the menstrual flow is consistent, conceiving is easy, and children often live long, as the moonlight gradually increases until full. However, if from the full moon to the new moon the menstrual flow fails to maintain its regularity, conception is difficult and many children face early death, mirroring the waning moonlight that diminishes and the moon's outline that becomes hollow. This is the principle of creation; can it be explained to the ignorant?

    石室秘录 【清　陈土铎】

    　　　　　子嗣论

    　　人生子嗣，虽曰天命，岂非人事哉！有男子不能生子者，有女子不能生子者。男子不能生子，有六病。女子不能生子，有十病。六病维何？一精寒也，一气衰也，一痰多也，一相火盛也，一精少也，一气郁也。精寒者，肾中之精寒，虽射入子宫，而女子胞胎不纳，不一月而即堕矣。气衰者，阳气衰也，气衰则不能久战，以动女子之欢心，男精已泄而女精未交，何能生物乎？精少者虽能射，而精必衰薄，胞胎之口大张，细小之入何能餍足？故随入而随出矣。[36p]

    The Secret Records of the Stone Chamber
    By Chen Tuduo, Qing Dynasty

    On Progeny

    To have offspring in life, although it is said to be a heavenly decree, is it not also a matter of human affairs? There are men who cannot father children, and women who cannot conceive. For men who cannot father children, there are six ailments. For women who cannot conceive, there are ten ailments. What are the six ailments? One is cold essence, one is declining energy, one is excess phlegm, one is excessive fiery essence, one is insufficient essence, and one is blocked energy. Cold essence refers to the coldness in the essence of the kidneys; even if it is released into the womb, the woman's body cannot accept it, and it will not be a month before it miscarries. Declining energy refers to the weakening of yang energy; when energy is low, one cannot engage in prolonged effort to stir the woman's heart; if the man's essence has already been emitted while the woman's essence has not yet mingled, how can life be conceived? Even if the essence is few and the man can still release it, it is certainly weak and thin, and when the womb's entrance opens wide, how can a small quantity satisfy? Therefore, it goes in and immediately comes out.[36p]

    痰多者，多湿也，多湿则精不纯，夹杂之精，总然生子，必然夭丧。相火盛者，过于久战，女精已过而男精未施，及男精既施而女兴已寝，又安能生育哉？气郁者，乃肝气抑塞，不能生心包之火，则怀抱忧愁，而阳事因之不振，或临炉而兴已阑，或对垒而戈忽倒，女子之春思正浓，而男子之浩叹顿起，则风景萧条，房帏岑寂，柴米之心难忘，调笑之言绝少，又何能种玉于蓝田，毓麟于兰室哉？故精寒者温其火，气衰者补其气，痰多者消其痰，火盛者补其水，精少者添其精，气郁者舒其气，则男子无手者可以有子，不可徒补其相火也。[37p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[37p]

    Those with excessive phlegm are often damp; excessive dampness leads to impure essence. If the essence is mixed, although conception may occur, the offspring is destined to perish. When the fire of vitality is strong and one endures prolonged battles, if the female essence has already passed while the male essence has yet to be released, and when the male essence is released but the female becomes quiescent, how can there be the prospect of reproduction? Stagnation of qi is due to the liver's energy being obstructed, unable to generate the heart’s warmth, leading to a harboring of worries, causing a lack of vigor in intimate matters. One may either have their joys extinguished or face sudden collapses; while women's springtime desires are strong, men's deep sighs arise. This results in desolate scenes, quiet rooms, an indelible longing for provisions, and scant laughter. How can one nurture jade in the blue fields or conceive a dragon in the fragrant chambers? Thus, for those with cold essence, warm their vitality; for those with weak qi, replenish their energy; for those with excessive phlegm, disperse it; for those with strong fire, nourish their water; for those with scant essence, augment their essence; and for those with stagnant qi, soothe their energy. This way, even men who feel powerless can still have offspring; merely supplementing the fire of vitality is not sufficient.[37p]

    十病维何？一胞胎冷也，一脾胃寒也，一带脉急也，一肝气郁也，一痰气盛也，一相火旺也，一肾水衰也，一任督病也，一膀胱气化不行也，一气血虚而不能摄也。胞胎之脉，所以受物者也，暖则生物，而冷则杀物矣。纵男子精热而射入之，又安能茹之而不吐乎？脾胃虚寒，则带脉之间，必然无力，精即射入于胞胎，又安能胜任乎？带脉宜迟不宜急。带脉急者，由于腰脐之不利也。腰脐不利，则胞胎无力，又安能载物乎？肝气郁则心境不舒，何能为欢于床第？痰气盛者，必肥妇也，毋论身肥则下体过胖，子宫缩入，难以受精，即或男子甚健，鼓勇而战，射精直入，而湿由膀胱，必有泛滥之虞。[38p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[38p]

    What are the ten diseases? One is cold in the womb, one is cold in the spleen and stomach, one is urgency in the dai vessel, one is stagnation of liver qi, one is excess of phlegm and qi, one is exuberance of fire, one is deficiency of kidney water, one is illness of the governor and conducive vessels, one is dysfunction in bladder qi transformation, and one is deficiency of qi and blood, unable to sustain life. The pulse of the womb is what receives substances; warmth allows for life, while cold leads to death. Even if a man's essence is hot and enters, how can it be retained without being expelled? If the spleen and stomach are weak and cold, then the dai vessel will naturally be powerless; if the essence enters the womb, how can it function properly? The dai vessel should be slow, not urgent. If the dai vessel is urgent, it is due to problems with the waist and navel. If there are problems with the waist and navel, the womb will be weak; how can it sustain anything? If liver qi is stagnant, the heart will be uncomfortable; how can there be joy in the marital bed? If phlegm and qi are excessive, it is likely due to obesity; regardless of body size, if the lower body is overly plump and the uterus is constricted, it will be difficult to conceive. Even if a man is very healthy, bravely fighting, and ejaculation occurs directly, if dampness arises from the bladder, there will surely be the risk of overflow.[38p]

    相火旺者，则过于焚烧焦干之地，又苦草木之难生。肾水衰者，则子宫燥涸，禾苗无雨露之润，亦成萎黄，必有堕贻之叹。任督之间，倘有疝瘕之证，则精不能施，因外有所障也。膀胱与胞胎相近，倘气化不行，则水湿之气。必且渗入于胞胎，而不能受妊矣。女子怀胎，必气血足而后能养，倘气虚则阳衰，血虚则阴衰，气血双虚则胞胎下坠而不能升举，小产之不能免也。故胞胎冷者温之，脾胃寒者暖之，带脉急者缓之，肝气郁者开之，痰气盛者消之，相火旺者平之，肾水衰者补之，任督病者除之，膀胱气化不行者助其肾气，气血不能摄胎者益其气血，则女子无子者亦可以有子，而不可徒治其胞胎也。[39p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[39p]

    Those with excessive fire disturbance burn and dry out the land, making it difficult for plants to grow. When kidney water is deficient, the uterus becomes dry, and seedlings lack the nourishing rain, leading to wilting and inevitable sorrow. If there are signs of hernia or blockage between the Ren and Du channels, the essence cannot be released, as it is obstructed externally. The bladder is close to the womb; if the transformation of qi is inefficient, the dampness will inevitably seep into the womb, preventing conception. For a woman to conceive, she must have ample qi and blood; if qi is deficient, yang declines, and if blood is deficient, yin declines. When both qi and blood are insufficient, the womb will sink and cannot rise, leading to miscarriage. Therefore, if the womb is cold, it must be warmed; if the spleen and stomach are cold, they need to be warmed; if the Dai vessel is tight, it should be relaxed; if liver qi is stagnant, it must be opened; if phlegm and qi are excessive, they need to be resolved; if fire is excessive, it should be balanced; if kidney water is deficient, it must be supplemented; if there are issues with the Ren and Du channels, they must be addressed; if bladder qi transformation is not functioning, support the kidney qi; if qi and blood cannot nourish the fetus, bolster the qi and blood. Thus, even women who are barren may conceive, and one cannot merely treat the womb in isolation.[39p]

    方

    Chengze Yuan treats thirty-six ailments of women’s lower abdomen, infertility, and cessation of childbirth.

    Meihuiren and Xin Yi, each one sheng; Sōushū, three taels; Gāoběn, one tael; Zélán, five he; and seven pieces of Gěshàngtíng.

    Grind the above into powder, and mix with honey to form pills the size of beans. Take two pills before meals, three times a day; if there’s no stagnation or accumulation in the abdomen, replace Gěshàngtíng with one tael of Tōngcǎo. Avoid licorice to harmonize the medicine; first use bitter wine to dissolve, then add a little honey to make into pills.

    Jincheng Tai Shou Bawei Yuan treats menstrual issues, blockage, and infertility. Taking this medicine for twenty-eight days will result in pregnancy.

    Ingredients: Baiwei, Xiǎoxīn, each thirty zhū; Rénshēn, Dùhén, Mǔméng, Hòubǐ, Bànxià, Bái jiāngcán, Dāngguì, Zǐwàn each eighteen zhū; Niúxī, Shāshēn, Gānjiāng, Qīnjiǎo each half a tael; Shūjiāo, Fùzǐ, Fángfēng each one and a half taels.

    Grind these into fine powder, mix with honey to make pills the size of wuzi. Initially take three pills, gradually increasing to four or five. This medicine should not be taken for a long time; once pregnancy is sensed, stop taking it—its effectiveness is significant.

    In one formula, use Mǔlì and omit Dùhén. In another formula, add Jiégěng and Dānsēn, each eighteen zhū.

    There is another prescription for prolonged infertility, or when there is a heat above and cold below, as well as all the ailments of women.[41p]

    The Great Yellow Pill treats dozens of ailments related to vaginal discharge and infertility.

    Five taels of Chuanxiong, with the Great Yellow crushed to the size of rice grains and boiled until black; one sheng each of Chaihu, (Shibai), saltpeter, and dry ginger; one piece of Poria the size of a chicken egg; two taels of Shu pepper.

    Grind these into a fine powder and form into honey pills the size of a walnut. Take seven pills before meals, wash down with rice wine, and gradually increase to ten pills, adjusting to what you feel comfortable with.

    After five days, there will be slight discharge; after ten days, blood will come out; after twenty days, long worms and yellowish-green fluid will be expelled; after thirty days, the illness will be cured; after fifty days, you will be healthy and plump.[44p]

    Purple quartz and Asparagus have an affinity for cold in the womb. Those who conceive often face difficulties; a woman may initially suffer from heart pain, which can lead to heart disease, and she may not experience her menstrual cycle. Taking this remedy can nourish and help her conceive.

    Ingredients include: 3 taels of purple quartz, Asparagus, and Yuyuliang; 2 taels each of herbs such as Ephedra, Aconite, Cistanche, Cinnamon heart, Licorice, Schisandra, Biota seed, Dendrobium, Ginseng, Alisma, Polygala, and Eucommia; 1 tael each of Sichuan pepper, rolling fern, mistletoe, ground heather, mica, Angelica, and fish bone.

    Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of a nut, taking 20 pills with wine, twice daily, up to 40 pills if necessary.

    This remedy is for treating women who have a cold constitution and lack heat, leading to prolonged infertility.

    To prepare, take 1 pound of Cyperus, process it into powder, and sift out the head powder. Use half a pound of the middle powder and soak it in wine with 3 taels each of white atractylodes (roasted) and Chinese angelica; 2 taels each of Chuanxiong, white peony, cooked and raw Rehmannia, white poria, moutan root (roasted), scutellaria, motherwort, and Bupleurum; and the white bark of the root of the stinking ash.

    Ai Fu Warm Palace Pills: Prepare as follows. Use six taels of香附 (xiang fu), five sheng of vinegar, and boil for a day and night in a clay jar. Pound into a paste, do not form into cakes, and slowly dry it over low heat. Use three taels each of 椒叶 (ai ye) and 当归 (dang gui), and half a tael of 续断 (xu duan); two taels each of 吴茱萸 (wu zhu yu), 川芎 (chuan xiong), and 炒白芍 (chao bai shao), and two taels of 黄芪 (huang qi); one tael of 生地 (sheng di) and five qian of 官桂 (guan gui). Mix these into a fine powder, add quality rice vinegar to form pills the size of a walnut. Take fifty to seventy pills, washed down with diluted vinegar soup. It is best to prepare on the day of Renzi or on days aligned with the virtues of the month and day, or on days conducive to life-prolonging energy, with utmost sincerity.

    Black Chicken Pills: These treat women's spleen and stomach deficiency, damage to the Chong and Ren vessels, insufficient blood and energy, and menstrual irregularities leading to infertility, with proven efficacy. Take a black-feathered, male, fat black-bone chicken, and feed it glutinous rice for seven days without allowing it to eat insects or field animals. After killing and plucking it, weigh it at a rate of one jin. Fill the chicken's belly with two taels each of 生地 (sheng di), 熟地 (shu di), 天冬 (tian dong), and 麦冬 (mai dong), and ten bowls of sweet, mellow wine. Boil in a sand pot until tender, then take it out, roast it over mulberry wood until the medicine is removed, and then soak it in the remaining wine until dry and charred. Use two taels each of 杜仲 (du zhong),炒归身 (chao gui shen), 川芎 (chuan xiong), 白术 (bai zhu), 丹参 (dan shen), and 茯苓 (fu ling); one tael each of 炒破故纸 (chao po gu zhi), 人参 (ren shen), 炙甘草 (zhi gan cao), and meat of 肉苁蓉 (rou cong rong) washed in wine to remove scales; and one tael of lightly roasted 小茴 (xiao hui) and 砂仁 (sha ren); and four taels of 香附子 (xiang fu zi) soaked in vinegar for three days and dried. Grind these together into powder, and mix with wine to form a dough for pills. Take fifty pills with warm empty wine or rice drink.[47p]

    补宫丸　固下元。

    Bum Gong Pill: Strengthening the Lower Origin

    White peony, stir-fried in wine,
    Chinese yam, dragon bone calcined,
    Red stone resin, all in equal parts,
    Dried ginger, stir-fried and reduced by half.
    Make into pills with vinegar paste and consume with hollow rice decoction.

    The formula for Yulin Pearl treats women with deficiency of blood and qi, irregular meridians, or experiences of intermittent flow, or discharges with dampness, or abdominal pain, or lower back soreness, or lack of appetite, and weakness with infertility. Taking one to two jin can lead to conception.

    Ingredients:

    • 2 liang each of ginseng, bai zhu roasted in earth, poria, and peony wine roasted
    • 1 liang each of chuan xiong and honey-fried licorice
    • 4 liang each of angelica, shud di wine steamed and crushed, and dodder seed prepared
    • 2 liang each of du zhong roasted and cut, deer antler powder, and chuan pepper

    Grind these ingredients into a powder. Form small pills the size of a pea, taking one or two pills on an empty stomach, with wine or plain water. Alternatively, they can be swallowed as small pills. If there is severe cold in the uterus, or if there are issues of diarrhea or pain, add prepared fuzi and roasted ginger as needed.[49p]

    加味六味地黄丸 【《准绳》，下同】 　妇人经事不调，即非受孕光景，纵使受之，亦不全美，宜服此丸。　　熟地黄四两　山茱萸肉　山药各二两　泽泻　香附米童便浸透，炒干三次，各一两　牡丹皮　白茯苓各一两五钱　蕲艾叶去筋酢煮，五钱　　右为末，炼蜜丸如梧子大，每服七十丸，百沸汤送下，随后证作汤使，或另作煎剂服。经水过期者，乃血虚也，宜四物汤知参、芪、陈皮，白朮服之。若肥白人是痰多，宜二陈加南星、苍朮、滑石、芎、归、香附之类。经水不及期者，血热也，四物加芩、连。肥人亦兼痰治。色紫黑者，同血热论。经将行而作疼者，气滞也，用归身尾、香附米及桃仁、红花、黄连以行之，或加四物、莪朮、延胡索、木香；热加黄芩、柴胡。经行后作疼者，血气虚也，八物汤。[50p]

    Enhanced Six-Flavor Rehmannia Pill

    For women whose menstruation is irregular, it is not necessarily due to pregnancy; even if they are pregnant, it may not be entirely perfected, thus they should take this pill.

    Ingredients:

    • 4 taels of prepared Rehmannia
    • 2 taels each of Cornelian Cherry fruit and Dioscorea
    • 1 tael each of Alisma, Cyperus (fried until dry three times),
    • 1.5 taels each of Peony root and White Poria
    • 0.5 taels of Qiying leaf (deveined and boiled in vinegar)

    Grind these into a powder and form into pills the size of a walnut; take seventy pills with boiling water. Following that, this can be made into a decoction or another infusion for consumption.

    For those whose menstrual flow is overdue, it indicates blood deficiency; they should take Four Substance Decoction with Radix Astragali, Tepal of Atractylodes, Chen Pi, and Bai Zhu.

    If the person is plump and pale, indicative of excess phlegm, additional ingredients like Erchen combined with Nanshan, Cangzhu, Talcum, Chuanxiong, and Cyperus should be included.

    If menstruation is overdue due to blood heat, then incorporate the following: add Huangqin and Lian to the Four Substance Decoction. Overweight individuals should also address phlegm treatment.

    If the color is dark purple, it's similar to the discussion of blood heat. If pain occurs just before menstruation, this indicates stagnation of qi; thus, ingredients like Gui Shenwei, Cyperus, Peach kernel, Safflower, and Coptis can be used to aid in relieving it, potentially adding Four Substance, Curcuma, Yanhusuo, and Mu Xiang; for heat, Huangqin and Chaihu should be added.

    If pain occurs post-menstruation, it indicates deficiency of blood and qi; Eight Substance Decoction should be employed.[50p]

    Regulating Menstruation Pill: Taking this will lead to having children.

    Ingredients: Half a pound of Xiangfu (Cyperus rotundus), one part of urine, one part of wine, and one part of vinegar, all soaked together; one part of raw material, all stir-fried with wine. Half a pound of Duzhong (Eucommia ulmoides) stir-fried with ginger juice; four taels each of Chuanxiong (Szechuan lovage), Donggui (Angelica sinensis), Qingpi (green tangerine peel), fried wheat, Baishao (white peony root), Shengdi (raw Rehmannia), Chenpi (dried tangerine peel), Xiao Hui Xiang (fennel), Wuyao (Lindera aggregata), Yan Huo Suo (Corydalis), stir-fried lightly, and Rou Cong Rong (Chinese dodder) soaked in wine; Huangqin (Scutellaria baicalensis) stir-fried in wine, all four taels.

    These fourteen ingredients should be weighed precisely with good materials. Mix vinegar with flour to form a paste and shape into pills the size of a sycamore seed. Take one hundred pills each time and wash them down with good wine on an empty stomach. If there are no Chenpi or Shengdi, one can use two taels each of Ginseng and Huangqi (Astragalus).

    Zhengyuan Dan: A seed for regulating menstruation.

    Ingredients: One pound of Xiangfu, combined with three taels of Ai Ye (mugwort), soaked together in vinegar for a night. Then mix each with four taels of wine, salt, and urine; two taels of Aijiao (donkey-hide gelatin) and clam powder stir-fried; four taels each of Shengdi washed with wine, and Zhihua (bitter orange peel) stir-fried partially with flour. Four taels each of Chuanxiong stir-fried and Donggui washed with wine, Shudi (cooked Rehmannia) soaked in wine; eight taels of Baishao, half raw and half stir-fried with wine.

    Grind these to a powder, mix with vinegar, and form pills the size of sycamore seeds. Swallow fifty to sixty pills with salty broth on an empty stomach. If there are any issues, add Bai Fuling (Poria) and Amber.[54p]

    永固孕汤 【《准绳》】 　常服固孕。　　地黄　川芎　黄芩各五分　归身尾　白芍药　人参　陈皮各一钱　白朮一钱　甘草三钱　桑上羊食藤圆者七叶，即金银藤　黄蘗少许　　右(口父)咀，入糯米四十粒，水煎服。

    Yonggu Yuntang (Formula for Supporting Pregnancy)

    For regular use to support pregnancy:

    • Each five grams of Rehmannia, Chuanxiong, and Scutellaria
    • Each ten grams of Angelica, White Peony, Ginseng, and Chenpi
    • Ten grams of Atractylodes
    • Thirty grams of Licorice
    • Seven leaves of the round variety of the mulberry plant, also known as Jin Yin Teng
    • A small amount of Huangbo

    Crush the above ingredients, add forty grains of glutinous rice, and decoct with water for consumption.

    Sitting-Guide Medicine

    For inability to conceive or recurrent miscarriages, take Qianjin Dangbao Decoction; if there are residual unhealthy substances, use this instead.

    • Two liang each of licorice, Shan Zhuyu, and Angelica
    • One liang each of Schisandra, Asarum (with roots removed), and processed dried ginger
    • Half liang each of white alum, rhubarb, Rong salt, and Sichuan pepper

    Grind these into a fine powder and pack tightly into a silk bag measuring about three inches long. Secure it, and place it inside the woman’s vagina. She may sit or lie down as she wishes, but should not walk. Remove it during urination and reinsert afterward.

    Change the bag once a day; it must be new. If done correctly, a clear yellow fluid will be discharged, and when it stops, intercourse can occur, leading to conception. If no symptoms are observed, it can be kept in place for up to ten days. This medicine is initially used to expel residual unhealthy substances from the uterus after using the Dangbao Decoction. The presence of cold residual substances in the uterus leads to infertility. In cold, damp weather, pain may occur; it is important to wait until the ailment subsides completely and not to discontinue prematurely.

    Every morning, for breakfast, use a decoction of bitter chicory to assist. The "Qianjin Yi" contains bitter gourd but not Shan Zhuyu.[55p]

    荡胞汤 【《千金方》】 　治妇人立身以来，全不产育；及断绪久不产，三十年者，宜服。　　附子炮，一两半　(石卜)硝　当归　大黄蒸一饭久　牡丹皮　桃仁去皮尖，各三两　厚朴姜汁炙　牛膝　桔梗　赤芍药　人参　茯苓　桂心　甘草炙　陈橘皮各二两　蝱虫去翅足，炒焦　水蛭炒，枯各十枚　　右十七件，以清酒五升，水六升，合煮取三分，分四服，日三夜一，每服相去三辰，更服。如常覆被，少时出汗。汗不出，冬月着火笼之。必下积血及冷赤脓，如赤小豆汁。本为妇人子宫内有此恶物令然，或天阴脐下痛，或月水不调，为有冷血不受胎。若斟酌下尽，气力弱，大困不堪，更服亦可，二三服即止。如大闷不堪，可食酢饮冷浆一口即止。然空去恶物不尽，不大得药力，若能忍服尽，大好。一日后仍着坐导药。一方有细辛二两。[56p]

    Dang Bao Tang (from "Thousand Gold Prescriptions")

    For women who have not conceived since their youth, and after a prolonged period of infertility, especially after thirty years, it is advisable to take this remedy.

    Ingredients:

    • Aconite (processed) 1.5 taels
    • Nitre (stone salt)
    • Angelica 3 taels
    • Rhubarb (steamed for a long time with rice)
    • Peony root 3 taels
    • Peach kernel (peeled and pointed) 3 taels
    • Magnolia bark with ginger juice, roasted
    • Achyranthes 2 taels
    • Platycodon 2 taels
    • Red peony 2 taels
    • Ginseng 2 taels
    • Poria 2 taels
    • Cinnamon heart 2 taels
    • Licorice (roasted) 2 taels
    • Aged tangerine peel 2 taels
    • Cattle tick (wings and legs removed, toasted until charred) 10 pieces
    • Leech (toasted and dried) 10 pieces

    Preparation: Combine the seventeen ingredients with 5 sheng of clear wine and 6 sheng of water, boil down to one third, and divide into four doses. Take three times during the day and once at night, spacing each dose by three "chen" (about 6 hours). When taking, cover warmly; if little sweat appears, use a fire box in winter. This will eliminate stagnant blood and cool, red pus, similar to red bean juice. This is meant for women whose uterus contains such harmful substances, which may cause pain below the navel during damp weather or irregular menstrual flow due to cold blood preventing conception. If symptoms worsen, with weakness and severe distress, it is permissible to take more doses; however, two to three doses should suffice. If the distress is overwhelming, a mouthful of vinegar with cold liquid may be taken to stop it. Nevertheless, if the harmful substances are not fully expelled, the medicinal power will not be fully realized; enduring the full treatment is ideal. After one day, continue to sit and guide the medicine. An alternate recipe may include 2 taels of Asarum.[56p]

    玉钥启荣丸 【《广嗣方》】 治妇人无子。　　香附子捣去毛，酢水浸三日，炒干细末，十五两　当归二两　白芍药　川芎　赤石脂　槁本　人参　牡丹皮　白茯苓　白薇　桂心　白芷　白朮　延胡索　没药各一两　　右除石脂、没药外，余药到，酒浸三日，焙干为末，足十五两，重罗极细，入别研赤石脂、没药末，炼蜜和丸弹子大，每取一丸，空心鸡未鸣时，先以温茶或薄荷汤漱口后细嚼，温酒或白汤送下，以干物压下，服至一月即效。按《医学入门》此方无桂心，有熟地黄，名女金丹。治妇人无子，或多痰火等疾。经候亦调，容颜不减，但久无孕，乃子宫有阴无阳，不能生发，宜服此鼓动微阳，一月即效。或赤白带下崩漏，及血风血气虚劳诸证，无所不治，真女中金丹也。[57p]

    Jade Key to the Glory Pill

    From "Expanded Succession Formulas"

    For treating women without children.

    Chuanxiong (ligusticum wallichii) and the others should be ground to remove hair; soak in vinegar water for three days, then roast and finely grind to powder—15 liang.

    Add 2 liang of Donggui (angelica sinensis), Bai Shao (white peony), Chuanxiong, Chi Shizhi (red resin), Jiao Ben (burnt herb), Ren Shen (ginseng), Mu Dan Pi (peony bark), Bai Fu Ling (white poria), Bai Wei (white nettle), Gui Xin (cinnamon heart), Bai Zhi (angelica), Bai Zhu (atractylodes), Yan Hu Suo (corydalis), and Mo Yao (myrrh) each 1 liang.

    Excluding Chi Shizhi and Mo Yao, the remaining herbs should be soaked in wine for three days, then roasted and powdered to a total of 15 liang. Sift finely and combine with separately ground Chi Shizhi and Mo Yao; then mix with honey and form into pills the size of a ball.

    Take one pill before dawn while the hens have not yet crowed, rinse the mouth with warm tea or mint decoction, chew thoroughly, and swallow with warm wine or plain water, pressed down with solid food.

    Take for one month for effect. According to "Medical Entry," this formula does not include Gui Xin but has熟地黄 (cooked rehmannia), called "Nü Jin Dan" (Women's Gold Pill).

    It treats women without children, or those with excessive phlegm and fire-related ailments. Observing the signs also adjusts conditions without diminishing appearance. However, prolonged absence of pregnancy indicates the uterus has yin but no yang, unable to generate.

    It is advisable to take this to stimulate slight yang; effects will appear in one month. For conditions like red and white discharge, metrorrhagia, blood wind, and blood qi deficiency, it is a universal remedy, truly the gold pill for women.[57p]

    Amber Regulating Menstruation Pill

    Treats women with cold womb lacking offspring, capable of regulating menstruation. Take one pound of fragrant cypress seeds, divided into two packages, soak each in rice vinegar for nine days. Mix with four taels of clean cooked mugwort and another five bowls of vinegar, then cook together in a clay pot until dry. Take one tael of amber, two taels each of Chuanxiong, Angelica, Peony, cooked and raw Rehmannia, and Myrrh. Grind these into a powder, mix with vinegar paste, and form into pills the size of walnuts. For every hundred pills, take them with a hollow center and swallow with mugwort vinegar soup.

    Enhanced Nourishing Pill

Also treats issues like fetal movement and leakage before birth, regular consumption can prevent miscarriage.     For treating the same issues.

    Ingredients:

    • One pound of Xiang Fu Mi (Cyperus), soaked in child’s urine, washed with water, dew-dried overnight, soaked, dew-dried, and sun-dried three times. Then soak overnight in good vinegar, dry, and grind to a powder.

    Regulating Menstrual and Nourishing Blood Pill

    2 qian of stir-fried fennel.

    Regulating Menstrual and Planting Seeds Decoction
    For women without children, often due to emotional distress affecting menstrual regulation, resulting in inability to conceive.

    6 qian each of steamed cooked Rehmannia and stir-fried Chuanxiong;
    3 qian each of washed Dong Quai, Wu Zhu Yu, and Chuanxiong;
    2 qian each of cinnamon and cooked mugwort.

Once the doses are finished, engage in intercourse, and conception is assured. This remedy is highly effective.[62p]

    Xiantian Guiyi Decoction
    Treats the aforementioned conditions.

    Acupuncture

    The "Jia Yi Jing" states: For women with severe hernias leading to infertility, treat them accordingly.
    For women facing infertility, moxibustion is applied to the navel to produce children.
    For women unable to bear children, the point at the front of the inner ankle is the primary treatment.
    For women who have never given birth, the Yinjian point should be the focus; insert the needle eight tenths of a cun, which is one inch below the sheep's marrow.
    The Shimen point, associated with the triple warmer, has various names including Liji, Jinglu, Dantian, and Mingmen, located two inches below the navel, where the Ren channel qi emerges.
    Women must not perform needling or moxibustion in the center, as this could lead to infertility.
    The "Mai Jing" states: The absence of the "Child Gate" pulse in the right wrist indicates infertility; this often results from cold reversals that prevent childbirth and lead to discharge without children.[64p]

    阴中寒，刺足少阴经治阴。　　《千金方》曰：女子不字，阴暴出，经漏，刺然谷，入三分，灸三壮，穴在足内踝前起大骨下陷中。　　拘挛腹满疝，月水不下，乳余疾绝子，阴痒，贲豚上(月真)，腹坚痛，下引阴中，不得小便，刺阴交入八分，灸五壮，穴在脐下一寸。　　绝子阴挺出，不禁自沥，刺上髎，入三寸，留七呼，灸三壮，穴在第一空腰髀下一寸侠脊。　　女子无子，咳而短气，刺涌泉，入三分，灸三壮，穴在足心陷者中。　　气冲主无子，小腹痛。[65p]

    In the cold of Yin, puncture the foot's Shao Yin channel to treat Yin. The "Thousand Gold Prescriptions" states: For women with irregular menstruation and abnormal discharge, puncture the Ren Guan point, penetrating three divisions, and apply moxibustion three times. The point lies in the depression below the prominent bone in front of the inner ankle. For cases of abdominal constriction, fullness, hernia, absence of menstrual flow, excessive milk leading to infertility, vaginal itching, and solid pain in the abdomen radiating downwards without urination, puncture the Yin Jiao point down to eight divisions, and apply moxibustion five times; the point is one inch below the navel. For infertility with protruding Yin not being contained, resulting in involuntary dripping, puncture the Shang Liao point to three inches deep, and leave it while taking seven breaths, moxibustion three times; the point is one inch below the first empty space, between the waist and hips. For women unable to conceive, with coughing and shortness of breath, puncture the Yong Quan point to three divisions and apply moxibustion three times; this point is located in the center of the depression on the sole of the foot. Qi stagnation leads to infertility, causing pain in the lower abdomen.[65p]

    水原、照海，主不字，阴暴出，淋漏，月水不来而多闷，心下痛。　　腹满疝积聚，乳余疾绝子，阴痒，奔豚上，少腹坚痛，下引阴中，不得小便，刺石门，入五分，穴在脐下二寸。忌灸，绝孕。　　绝子，衃血在内不下，胞转不得尿，小腹满，石水痛，刺关元，入二寸，灸七壮，穴在脐下三寸是也。　　子门不端，小腹疝，苦寒，阴痒及痛，贲豚抢心，饥不能食，腹胀，经闭不通，小便不利，乳余疾绝子，内不足，刺中极，入二寸，留十呼，灸三壮，穴在脐下四寸。　　女子疝瘕血闭，无子，不嗜食，刺曲泉，在膝内辅骨下大筋上小筋下陷中，屈膝乃得之。刺入六分，灸三壮。　　妇人无子，灸四满三十壮，穴在丹田两边相去各开寸半。丹田在脐下二寸是也。[66p]

    In the Water Source and the Reflecting Sea, the master does not write. The Yin violently exits, leaking and dripping; the moon's water does not come and feels heavy, causing pain in the heart.

    The abdomen is full with hernia and accumulation; leftover milk prevents childbirth; there is itching in the Yin region, a rushing sensation upwards, hard pain in the lower abdomen, leading to a difficulty in urination. Insert the needle at the Stone Gate, one-fifth deep; the point is two inches below the navel. Avoid moxibustion, as it will prevent pregnancy.

    For childbirth prevention, if blood is trapped inside and does not exit, causing the womb to be unable to pass urine, and with a full lower abdomen and stone-like pain, needle the Gate of Source, inserting two inches deep, then apply moxibustion for seven sessions; the point is three inches below the navel.

    If the Child Gate is not upright, and with hernia and cold pain in the lower abdomen, along with itching and pain, rushing in the heart, unable to eat due to hunger, abdominal distention, menstrual obstruction, and difficulty in urination: for leftover milk that prevents childbirth and internal insufficiency, needle the Middle Pole, inserting two inches deep, leave the needle for ten breaths, and apply moxibustion for three sessions; the point is four inches below the navel.

    For women with hernias, blood obstruction, and no children, having no appetite: needle the Ququan point, located in the middle of the lower muscle beneath the large muscle in the knee; this can be found by bending the knee. Insert six-tenths deep and apply moxibustion for three sessions.

    For a woman with no children, apply moxibustion thirty times at four points, each one and a half inches away from the Lower Elixir Field. The Lower Elixir Field is two inches below the navel.[66p]

    妇人绝子，灸然谷五十壮，穴在内踝前直下一寸。　　妇人绝嗣不生，胞门闭塞，灸关元三十壮，报之。　　妇人妊子不成，堕落，腹痛，漏见赤，灸胞门五十壮。　　妇人子脏闭塞，不受精疼，灸胞门五十壮。　　妇人绝嗣不生，灸气门五十壮，穴在关元旁三寸。　　妇人绝嗣不生，漏赤白，灸泉门十壮，三报，穴在横骨当阴上际。　　《东垣十书》曰：妇人无子，灸关元穴二十壮，三报。　　女人胞胎门落颓不收，常湿，灸神阙、玉泉各五十壮；身交灸五十壮，三报，穴在脐下横缝中。　　又法：玉泉旁开三寸，灸随年壮，三报。　　《医学纲目》曰：妇人无子，子宫针入二寸，灸三七壮，穴在中极旁各开三寸。　　《医学入门》曰：妇人针灸石门，终身孕不成。　　妇人中极灸三遍，令生子。[67p]

    A woman who cannot have children should apply moxibustion at the Guanyuan point for fifty applications, located one inch directly below the inner ankle. A woman who cannot conceive or has a blocked uterus should apply moxibustion at the Caomen point for thirty applications, to relieve the condition. A woman experiencing miscarriages, abdominal pain, and unusual bleeding should apply moxibustion at the Caomen point for fifty applications. If a woman’s uterus is obstructed and she suffers pain from infertility, she should apply moxibustion at the Caomen point for fifty applications. For women who cannot conceive and are experiencing white or red discharge, moxibustion should be applied at the Quanmen point for ten applications, three times, located three inches to the side of the Guanyuan point.

    According to the "Ten Books of Dongyuan": If a woman is childless, apply moxibustion at the Guanyuan point for twenty applications, three times. If the woman’s uterus is weak and lacks firmness, leading to excess moisture, apply moxibustion at the Shendi and Yinquan points for fifty applications each; apply moxibustion around the body for fifty applications, three times, with the points located in the horizontal seam beneath the navel.

    Another method involves opening three inches from the Yinquan point and applying moxibustion based on age, three times. According to the "Medical Principles": If a woman is childless, insert a needle two inches into the uterus and apply moxibustion for thirty-seven applications, with the points located three inches on either side of the Zhongji point. The "Introduction to Medicine" states that if a woman receives acupuncture at the Shimen point, she will remain barren for life. Moxibustion should be applied three times at the Zhongji point to promote childbirth.[67p]

    三阴交，治妇人久不成孕。
    　　《古今医鉴》曰：妇人子宫冷甚不孕，灸丹田七壮，神效，穴在脐下三寸。何以知其冷甚？丈夫交会之际，当自知之也。　　女人无孕，或经生子后久不成孕。及怀孕不成，用秆心一条，长十四寸，令女人仰卧，舒手足以所量秆心，自脐心直垂下尽头处，以墨点记后，以此秆心平折，横安前点处两头尽处是穴，按之自有动脉应手，各灸三七壮，炷如箸头，神验。即胞门子户穴也。[68p]

    San Yin Jiao is used to treat women who have difficulty conceiving for a long time.

    The "Medical Reference of Past and Present" states: When a woman's uterus is extremely cold, she cannot conceive. Moxibustion should be applied to the lower abdomen seven times, which is highly effective. The acupuncture point is located three inches below the navel. How do we know it is extremely cold? The husband should be aware during the act of intercourse.

    If a woman has no pregnancy, or if it has been a long time since giving birth without conceiving again, she can use a stick measuring fourteen inches in length. The woman should lie on her back, stretch her arms and legs out to measure the stick, dropping it straight down from the navel's center to the end of the stick, marking this point with ink.

    Then, the stick should be bent horizontally, and the ends of the two sections should be placed at the marked point. Pressing there, one can feel the pulse respond. Each point should be treated with moxibustion three times, using moxa the size of a chopstick head, for significant effect. This is also the point associated with the entrance and exit of the uterus.[68p]

    医案

    　　《儒门事亲》曰：戴人过谯郡营中饮会，有一卒说黜妻事，戴人问其故，答曰：吾归为室女时，心下有冷积如覆杯，按之如水声，以热手熨之如冰，娶来已十五年矣，恐断吾嗣，故欲黜之。戴人曰：勿黜也，如用吾药，病可除，孕可得。卒从之。戴人诊其寸脉沉而迟，尺脉洪大有力，非无子之候也。可不踰年而孕。先以三圣散吐涎一斗，心下平软；次服白朮调中汤、五芩散；后以四物汤和之。不再月，气血合度，数月而娠一子。戴人常曰：吾用此法，无不子之妇。信不诬也。[69p]

    Medical Case

    The "Rumen Shiqin" states: A man named Dai was attending a drinking party in Qiao County when a soldier mentioned dismissing his wife. Dai inquired about the reason, to which the soldier replied: "When I returned home as a bride, there was a chill in my heart, like a covered cup. When pressed, it sounded like water; when warmed by my hand, it felt like ice. It has been fifteen years since we married, and I fear that I may have no heirs, hence I wish to dismiss her." Dai said: "Do not dismiss her; if you use my medicine, the illness can be cured, and you may achieve pregnancy." The soldier followed his advice. Dai diagnosed the soldier's pulse to be deep and slow, while the pulse at the wrist was strong and forceful, indicating that he was not without the potential for children. He could likely conceive within the year. First, he prescribed San Sheng San to induce vomiting of a bucket of phlegm and to soften the area of the heart. Next, he administered Baizhu Tiaozhong Decoction and Wuqin San; afterward, he mixed in Siwu Decoction. Within two months, the energies and blood harmonized, and after several months, he conceived a son. Dai often said: "With this method, no woman is without children." This is truly not a falsehood.[69p]

    《寓意草》曰：一友继室夫人，身体肥盛，经候虽调，从未孕育，令仆定方而施转移化机之药，虽从古医书所未载，然可得言也。盖山之不可葬者五，童断过石独，纵有明师，无所施其剪裁，以故女之不可孕。如方书所志，生禀之殊，非人工所能改移者，可不更论。若夫生禀不殊，但为形躯所累，而嗣孕终不乏者，古今来不知凡几。但夫妇之愚，天然凑合之妙，虽圣神有不能传者，所以方书阙焉未备耳。仆试言之：地之体本厚重，然得天气以包举之，则生机不息。若重阴冱寒之区，天日之光不显，则物生实罕。人之体中肌肉丰盛，乃血之荣旺，极为美事，但血旺易至气衰。[70p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[70p]

    The "Yuyi Cao" states: A friend’s wife, although her body is robust and well-proportioned, has, despite careful attention to her condition, never been able to conceive. So I instructed a servant to prepare a remedy for her, one that has not been recorded in ancient medical texts, but can certainly be discussed. There are five reasons why a mountain cannot be buried: if a child is blocked by a stone, even with a wise teacher, there is no way to apply the necessary measures; hence, a girl cannot conceive. As written in the medical texts, if one’s natural constitution is different, it cannot be changed by human effort, thus needing no further discussion. However, in cases where the natural constitution is not different but hindered by bodily issues, there are countless instances, both ancient and modern, of successful pregnancies. Yet, the foolishness of couples, the natural harmony that makes them compatible, even the most skilled cannot guarantee fertility, and thus the medical texts are lacking in this regard. I propose that the essence of the earth is inherently substantial, yet it relies on the influence of weather for vitality to persist. In areas of heavy cold and dampness, where sunlight fails to shine, life rarely thrives. The human body, rich in muscle and full of blood, is a beautiful thing; however, when blood is abundant, it can easily lead to a depletion of vital energy.[70p]

    夫气与血两相维附，何以偏衰偏旺耶？盖气为主则血流，血为主则气反不流，气不流有似于衰耳。所以一切补气之药皆不可用，而耗气之药反有可施，缘气得补则愈锢，不若耗之以助其流动之势，久则血仍归其统握之中耳。湖阳公主体肥受孕，不能产，得明者定一伤胎之方，服数十剂而临产始得顺利，母子俱安。盖肥满之躯，胎处其中，全无空隙，以故伤胎之药，止能耗其外之血肉，而不能耗其内之真元。仆仿是意而制方，豫为受胎之地。夫岂无术而杜撰乎？女之宜男者，先平其心，心和则气和，气和则易于流动充满也。其次在节食，仙府清肌，恒存辟谷，宫中细腰，得之忍饥，志壹动气，何事不成耶？而且为齐心杠德，以神道之教，补药饵之不逮，有不天人叶应者乎？仆于合浦求珠，蓝田种玉之举而乐道之。
    [71p]

    Reasoning Trace

    This is a placeholder for a reasoning trace of the translation, describing in detail how the translation was created.[71p]

    The interaction between qi and blood is intricate; how can one be weak or strong while the other is not? Qi is the master, thus blood flows; when blood is dominant, qi does not flow properly. When qi ceases to flow, it resembles a decline. Therefore, all medications that tonify qi should not be used, while those that drain qi might be beneficial, as nourishing qi could cause stagnation. It is better to reduce it to facilitate its movement, and over time, blood will return to its proper control.

    When Duke Huayang became pregnant but could not give birth due to excessive body weight, a knowledgeable person prescribed a method harmful to the fetus, and after taking several doses, she was able to deliver smoothly, ensuring the safety of both mother and child. Due to her plump body, the fetus had no space, so the medications merely drained the external flesh and blood but could not exhaust the true essence within.

    I formulated a prescription based on this understanding, preparing for the ideal conditions for conception. Is it not a skill to create? For a woman with a suitable partner, she must first calm her heart; a tranquil heart leads to harmonious qi, and harmonious qi is conducive to flowing and filling. Next, she should regulate her diet, maintaining a clean physique, often practicing fasting to achieve a slender waist in the womb, tolerating hunger and focusing her will to move qi; what can’t be accomplished with such effort?

    Moreover, by aligning hearts and nurturing virtue, and through the teachings of spiritual paths, can even tonics fall short? I seek pearls in Hepu and find joy in cultivating jade in Lantian.[71p]
